	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml') != '2262a95c43376fe5a4cd3052c6e39068f629afbf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml') !== '2262a95c43376fe5a4cd3052c6e39068f629afbf') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml') !== 'c34eeae6cfdf82d564184bf759375e61711b8e61') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml') !== '2262a95c43376fe5a4cd3052c6e39068f629afbf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/captcha/vts_challenge/manifest.xml');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '0134a160ea74d29f9bcafc994d9b524cd0d9c6a9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '0134a160ea74d29f9bcafc994d9b524cd0d9c6a9') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'b0a2585eb3cb0793890bee56e17e4ecc468da93a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '0134a160ea74d29f9bcafc994d9b524cd0d9c6a9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
